	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Iraqi Kurdistan</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This article is about the Kurdish populated areas in Iraq. For the autonomous entity, see <a href="/wiki/Kurdistan_Region" title="Kurdistan Region">Kurdistan Region</a>.</div>
<p>
<b>Iraqi Kurdistan</b> or <b>Southern Kurdistan</b><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> (<a href="/wiki/Kurdish_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Kurdish language">Kurdish</a>: <span lang="ku" dir="rtl">باشووری کوردستان</span>&#8206;, <small>romanized:&#160;</small><i lang="ku-Latn" title="Kurdish-language romanization">Başûrê Kurdistanê</i>) is the Kurdish-populated region incorporated into <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> and considered by <a href="/wiki/Kurds" title="Kurds">Kurds</a> as one of four parts of Greater <a href="/wiki/Kurdistan" title="Kurdistan">Kurdistan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Much of the geographical and cultural region of Iraqi Kurdistan is governed by the <b><a href="/wiki/Kurdistan_Region" title="Kurdistan Region">Kurdistan Region</a> (KRI)</b> (<a href="/wiki/Kurdish_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Kurdish language">Kurdish</a>: <span lang="ku" dir="rtl">هه‌رێمی کوردستان</span>&#8206;, <small>romanized:&#160;</small><i lang="ku-Latn" title="Kurdish-language romanization">Herêmî Kurdistan</i>) which is an <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_administrative_division" title="Autonomous administrative division">autonomous region</a> recognized by the Iraqi constitution.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:312px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ethnoreligious_Iraq.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Ethnoreligious_Iraq.svg/310px-Ethnoreligious_Iraq.svg.png" decoding="async" width="310" height="316" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Ethnoreligious_Iraq.svg/465px-Ethnoreligious_Iraq.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Ethnoreligious_Iraq.svg/620px-Ethnoreligious_Iraq.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1241" data-file-height="1264" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ethnoreligious_Iraq.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Map Ethnic and religious groups in Iraq<br /> <div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #eeffaa; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Kurds_in_Iraq" title="Kurds in Iraq">Muslim and Yarsan Kurds</a></div> <div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #cdde87; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Yazidis" title="Yazidis">Yazidis</a></div></div></div></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:262px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hewler-Kurdistan.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Hewler-Kurdistan.jpg/260px-Hewler-Kurdistan.jpg" decoding="async" width="260" height="133" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Hewler-Kurdistan.jpg/390px-Hewler-Kurdistan.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Hewler-Kurdistan.jpg/520px-Hewler-Kurdistan.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2054" data-file-height="1053" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hewler-Kurdistan.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Erbil" title="Erbil">Erbil</a>, capital of Iraqi Kurdistan</div></div></div>
<p>The exact origins of the name <i>Kurd</i> are unclear. The <a href="/wiki/Suffix" title="Suffix">suffix</a> <b>-<i>stan</i></b> (<a href="/wiki/Persian_language" title="Persian language">Persian</a>: ـستان‎, <small><a href="/wiki/Romanization_of_Persian" title="Romanization of Persian">translit.</a></small> <i>stân</i>) is <a href="/wiki/Persian_language" title="Persian language">Persian</a> for region. Literal translation "Region of Kurds".
</p><p>"Kurdistan" was also formerly spelled <i>Curdistan</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> One of the ancient names of Kurdistan is <i><a href="/wiki/Corduene" title="Corduene">Corduene</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-A.D._Lee,_1991_pp._366–374_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A.D._Lee,_1991_pp._366–374-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><span id="Background"></span>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">Geography</span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_Kurdistan" class="mw-redirect" title="Geography of Kurdistan">Geography of Kurdistan</a></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sulamani-kurdistan_(3).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Sulamani-kurdistan_%283%29.jpg/220px-Sulamani-kurdistan_%283%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="138" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Sulamani-kurdistan_%283%29.jpg/330px-Sulamani-kurdistan_%283%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Sulamani-kurdistan_%283%29.jpg/440px-Sulamani-kurdistan_%283%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1257" data-file-height="787" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sulamani-kurdistan_(3).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Lake_Dukan" title="Lake Dukan">Lake Dukan</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Greater_Zab_River_near_Erbil_Iraqi_Kurdistan.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Greater_Zab_River_near_Erbil_Iraqi_Kurdistan.jpg/220px-Greater_Zab_River_near_Erbil_Iraqi_Kurdistan.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Greater_Zab_River_near_Erbil_Iraqi_Kurdistan.jpg/330px-Greater_Zab_River_near_Erbil_Iraqi_Kurdistan.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Greater_Zab_River_near_Erbil_Iraqi_Kurdistan.jpg/440px-Greater_Zab_River_near_Erbil_Iraqi_Kurdistan.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2048" data-file-height="1536" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Greater_Zab_River_near_Erbil_Iraqi_Kurdistan.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Greater_Zab_River" class="mw-redirect" title="Greater Zab River">Greater Zab River</a> near Erbil</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:223px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Canyon,_north_eastern_Kurdistan.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Canyon%2C_north_eastern_Kurdistan.jpg/221px-Canyon%2C_north_eastern_Kurdistan.jpg" decoding="async" width="221" height="166" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Canyon%2C_north_eastern_Kurdistan.jpg/332px-Canyon%2C_north_eastern_Kurdistan.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Canyon%2C_north_eastern_Kurdistan.jpg/442px-Canyon%2C_north_eastern_Kurdistan.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3000" data-file-height="2250" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Canyon,_north_eastern_Kurdistan.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A canyon near the northern city of <a href="/wiki/Rawandiz" title="Rawandiz">Rawandiz</a></div></div></div>
<p>The Kurdistan Region is largely mountainous, with the highest point being a 3,611 m (11,847&#160;ft) point known locally as <a href="/wiki/Cheekha_Dar" title="Cheekha Dar">Cheekha Dar</a> ("black tent"). Mountains in Iraqi Kurdistan include the <a href="/wiki/Zagros" class="mw-redirect" title="Zagros">Zagros</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sinjar_Mountains" title="Sinjar Mountains">Sinjar Mountains</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hamrin_Mountains" title="Hamrin Mountains">Hamrin Mountains</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mount_Nisir" title="Mount Nisir">Mount Nisir</a> and <a href="/wiki/Qandil_mountains" class="mw-redirect" title="Qandil mountains">Qandil mountains</a>. There are many rivers running through the region, which is distinguished by its fertile lands, plentiful water, and picturesque nature. The <a href="/wiki/Great_Zab" title="Great Zab">Great Zab</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Little_Zab" title="Little Zab">Little Zab</a> flow from the east to the west in the region. The <a href="/wiki/Tigris" title="Tigris">Tigris</a> river enters Iraqi Kurdistan from <a href="/wiki/Turkish_Kurdistan" title="Turkish Kurdistan">Turkish Kurdistan</a>.
</p><p>The mountainous nature of Iraqi Kurdistan, the difference of temperatures in its various parts, and its wealth of waters make it a land of agriculture and tourism. The largest lake in the region is <a href="/wiki/Lake_Dukan" title="Lake Dukan">Lake Dukan</a>. There are also several smaller lakes, such as Darbandikhan Lake and Duhok Lake. The western and southern parts of the Kurdistan Region are not as mountainous as the east. Instead, it is rolling hills and <a href="/wiki/Plains" class="mw-redirect" title="Plains">plains</a> vegetated by <a href="/wiki/Sclerophyll" title="Sclerophyll">sclerophyll</a> scrubland.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ecology">Ecology</span></h3>
<p>Vegetation in the region includes, <a href="/wiki/Abies_cilicica" title="Abies cilicica">Abies cilicica</a>, <a href="/wiki/Quercus_calliprinos" title="Quercus calliprinos">Quercus calliprinos</a>, <a href="/wiki/Quercus_brantii" title="Quercus brantii">Quercus brantii</a>, <a href="/wiki/Quercus_infectoria" title="Quercus infectoria">Quercus infectoria</a>, <a href="/wiki/Quercus_ithaburensis" title="Quercus ithaburensis">Quercus ithaburensis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Quercus_macranthera" title="Quercus macranthera">Quercus macranthera</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cupressus_sempervirens" title="Cupressus sempervirens">Cupressus sempervirens</a>, <a href="/wiki/Platanus_orientalis" title="Platanus orientalis">Platanus orientalis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pinus_brutia" title="Pinus brutia">Pinus brutia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Juniperus_foetidissima" title="Juniperus foetidissima">Juniperus foetidissima</a>, <a href="/wiki/Juniperus_excelsa" title="Juniperus excelsa">Juniperus excelsa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Juniperus_oxycedrus" title="Juniperus oxycedrus">Juniperus oxycedrus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Salix_alba" title="Salix alba">Salix alba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Olea_europaea" class="mw-redirect" title="Olea europaea">Olea europaea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ficus_carica" class="mw-redirect" title="Ficus carica">Ficus carica</a>, <a href="/wiki/Populus_euphratica" title="Populus euphratica">Populus euphratica</a>, <a href="/wiki/Populus_nigra" title="Populus nigra">Populus nigra</a>, <a href="/wiki/Crataegus_monogyna" title="Crataegus monogyna">Crataegus monogyna</a>, <a href="/wiki/Crataegus_azarolus" title="Crataegus azarolus">Crataegus azarolus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cherry_plum" title="Cherry plum">cherry plum</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rose_hip" title="Rose hip">rose hips</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pistachio_tree" class="mw-redirect" title="Pistachio tree">pistachio trees</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pyrus_elaeagrifolia" title="Pyrus elaeagrifolia">pear</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sorbus_graeca" title="Sorbus graeca">Sorbus graeca</a>. The desert in the south is mostly <a href="/wiki/Steppe" title="Steppe">steppe</a> and would feature <a href="/wiki/Xeric" class="mw-redirect" title="Xeric">xeric</a> plants such as <a href="/wiki/Arecaceae" title="Arecaceae">palm trees</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tamarix" title="Tamarix">tamarix</a>, <a href="/wiki/Date_palm" title="Date palm">date palm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fraxinus" title="Fraxinus">fraxinus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Poa" title="Poa">poa</a>, <a href="/wiki/White_wormwood" class="mw-redirect" title="White wormwood">white wormwood</a> and <a href="/wiki/Chenopodiaceae" class="mw-redirect" title="Chenopodiaceae">chenopodiaceae</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Animals found in the region include the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_brown_bear" title="Syrian brown bear">Syrian brown bear</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wild_boar" title="Wild boar">wild boar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gray_wolf" class="mw-redirect" title="Gray wolf">gray wolf</a>, <a href="/wiki/Golden_jackal" title="Golden jackal">golden jackal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Indian_crested_porcupine" title="Indian crested porcupine">Indian crested porcupine</a>, <a href="/wiki/Red_fox" title="Red fox">red fox</a>, <a href="/wiki/Goitered_gazelle" title="Goitered gazelle">goitered gazelle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eurasian_otter" title="Eurasian otter">Eurasian otter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Striped_hyena" title="Striped hyena">striped hyena</a>, <a href="/wiki/Persian_fallow_deer" title="Persian fallow deer">Persian fallow deer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Onager" title="Onager">onager</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mangar_(fish)" title="Mangar (fish)">mangar</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Euphrates_softshell_turtle" title="Euphrates softshell turtle">Euphrates softshell turtle</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Bird species include, the <a href="/wiki/See-see_partridge" title="See-see partridge">see-see partridge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Menetries%27s_warbler" title="Menetries&#39;s warbler">Menetries's warbler</a>, <a href="/wiki/Western_jackdaw" title="Western jackdaw">western jackdaw</a>, <a href="/wiki/Red-billed_chough" title="Red-billed chough">Red-billed chough</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hooded_crow" title="Hooded crow">hooded crow</a>, <a href="/wiki/European_nightjar" title="European nightjar">European nightjar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rufous-tailed_scrub_robin" title="Rufous-tailed scrub robin">rufous-tailed scrub robin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Masked_shrike" title="Masked shrike">masked shrike</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Pale_rockfinch" title="Pale rockfinch">pale rockfinch</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">Climate</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Erbil_governorate_shanidar_cave.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Erbil_governorate_shanidar_cave.jpg/220px-Erbil_governorate_shanidar_cave.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="151" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Erbil_governorate_shanidar_cave.jpg/330px-Erbil_governorate_shanidar_cave.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Erbil_governorate_shanidar_cave.jpg/440px-Erbil_governorate_shanidar_cave.jpg 2x" data-file-width="749" data-file-height="515" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Erbil_governorate_shanidar_cave.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Shanidar_Cave" title="Shanidar Cave">Shanidar Cave</a>, surrounded by <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_vegetation" class="mw-redirect" title="Mediterranean vegetation">Mediterranean vegetation</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Due to its latitude and altitude, Iraqi Kurdistan is cooler and much wetter than the rest of Iraq. Most areas in the region fall within the <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_climate" title="Mediterranean climate">Mediterranean climate</a> zone (<i>Csa</i>), with areas to the southwest being <a href="/wiki/Semi-arid" class="mw-redirect" title="Semi-arid">semi-arid</a> (<i>BSh</i>). Due to the summers being less extreme, thousands of tourists from the hotter parts of Iraq <a href="/wiki/Summer_capital" title="Summer capital">come to visit the region in that season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite its reputation for having "mild" summers, they are still very hot for non-Iraqi standards though, with average temperatures ranging from 35&#160;°C (95&#160;°F) in the cooler northernmost areas to blistering 40&#160;°C (104&#160;°F) in the southwest, with lows around 21&#160;°C (70&#160;°F) to 24&#160;°C (75&#160;°F). Winters, however, are dramatically cooler than other areas in Iraq, with highs averaging between 9&#160;°C (48&#160;°F) and 11&#160;°C (52&#160;°F) and with lows hovering around 3&#160;°C (37&#160;°F) in some areas and <a href="/wiki/Freezing" title="Freezing">freezing</a> in others, dipping to −2&#160;°C (28&#160;°F) and 0&#160;°C (32&#160;°F) on average. Elevated places such as mountain tops would be colder.
</p><p>Among other cities in the climate table below, <a href="/wiki/Soran,_Iraq" title="Soran, Iraq">Soran</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shaqlawa" title="Shaqlawa">Shaqlawa</a> and <a href="/wiki/Halabja" title="Halabja">Halabja</a> also experience lows which average below 0&#160;°C (32&#160;°F) in winter. <a href="/wiki/Duhok" title="Duhok">Duhok</a> has the hottest summers in the region with highs averaging around 42&#160;°C (108&#160;°F). Annual rainfall contrasts in the region, with some places seeing rainfall as low as 500 millimetres (20&#160;in) in Erbil to as high as 900 millimetres (35&#160;in) in places like Amadiya. Most of the rain falls in winter and spring, and it's usually heavy. Summer and early autumn are virtually dry. Spring is fairly tepid. Iraqi Kurdistan sees <a href="/wiki/Snowfall" class="mw-redirect" title="Snowfall">snowfall</a> occasionally in the winter, and <a href="/wiki/Frost" title="Frost">frost</a> is very common. There is a <a href="/wiki/Seasonal_lag" title="Seasonal lag">seasonal lag</a> in some places in summer, with temperatures peaking around August and September.
</p>
